European Core (formerly: Community) Health Indicators (ECHI)initiative started 1998 project responding European Commission (EC)s call establish ashortlist public health indicator would serve core European public health monitoring system. first version theECHIshortlist wa approved theECand theEUMember States(MS)in 2005. 2008, theECand theEUMS began putting indicator practice. current shortlist contains 88 indicatorsgrouped five main chaptersand mapped 17 (non-exclusive) policy areas.Currently, 67 put practice (implemented). TheECHIwork ha coordinated series offiveECfunded projects:ECHI-I,ECHI-II,ECHIM,JAECHIM. TheBRIDGE Health project(2015-2018)and Joint Action Health Information (2018-2021) suggested improvement ECHI. TheECHIIndicators derive data variety sources, including theEU's statistical office (Eurostat), World Health Organisations European Health database (HFA-DB), Health Statistics database Organisation Economic Co-operation Development (OECD) several topic-specific databases. ECHI DOCUMENTATION Original ECHI report ECHI related report ) ECHIdata tool TheEuropean Commission Directorate Health Food SafetyDG SANTEestablished agraphic tool interactive application present relevant comparable information health European level, the. Source: Irene Kesisoglou, Shona Cosgrove, Pascal Derycke, Petronille Bogaert, Annika Jacobsen, Marco Roos, Anna Niemeyer, Alicia Martinez Garcia, Adrian Thorogood, Petr Holub, Irene Schluender, Salvador Capella-Gutierrez, Juan Gonzalez Garcia, Celia Alvarez Romero, Teresa D'Altri, Amy Curwin, Laura Portell Silva, & Lidia Lpez Cuesta. (2022). Glossary commonly used term field health data research - developed EU project HealthyCloud (1.0). Zenodo. GLOSSARY Aggregated data: Aggregated data pooled data. Statistical data several individual combined show general trend value within data.Aggregated data necessarily anonymised data. Anonymisation: processing personal data manner personal data longer attributed specific data subject. Removing personally identifiable information, definitively allow identification data subjects.The method used anonymise data context dependent. Cloud: Network computing facility providing remote data storage processing service internet. Cloud computing: Paradigm enabling network access scalable elastic pool shareable physical virtual resource administration on-demand. Comparative population health research: Comparisons health status, determinant service use across countries, and/or time. Consent: individual agreement e.g. participate research, undergo healthcare procedure, personal data processing. Within context personal data, GDPR defines consent as: freely given, specific, informed unambiguous indication data subject's wish she, statement clear affirmative action, signifies agreement processing personal data relating her. Data:Discrete observation attribute event carry little meaning considered alone Data defined recorded factual material commonly accepted scientific community information required support research findings. Refers digital representation acts, fact information compilation acts, fact information, including form sound, visual audiovisual recording. four major categorical type data data come from: observational; experimental; simulated derived. Data information available processing. Data access: processing data data user, wa provided data holder, accordance specific technical, legal, organisational requirements, without necessarily implying transmission downloading data. Data access right: ability, right permission act data defined location. Data altruism: Consent data subject process personal data pertaining them, permission data holder allow use non-personal data without seeking reward, purpose general interest, scientific research purpose improving public services. Data centric health research computational infrastructure: infrastructure provides data service. infrastructure includes services, data visualisation, hosting processing data. particular, canprocess health-related sensitive data. Technological infrastructure data analysis, exploitation and/or processing. Data controller: Regulation (EU) 2018/1725, well GDPR, data controller party that, alone jointly others, determines purpose mean processing personal data. actual processing may delegated another party, called data processor. controller responsible lawfulness processing, protection data, respecting right data subject. controller also entity receives request data subject exercise rights. Data curator:A person responsible quality FAIRness health-related data, make sure value data discovered accessible. role also considers possibility enriching data increasing quality. Importantly, data curator might play role regarding processors, e.g. responsible data hand. Data discoverability: ability mechanism browse locate available data relevant specific user purpose (e.g., research project) non-targeted search. Data discoverable data collection ha metadata metadata publicly accessible. Discoverability related findability FAIR principles. Data model: distributed research infrastructure, data model formal description data source (entities, attribute relationships) metadata specific scientific study, basis semantic interoperability, thus allowing reliable comparative research. Data governance: Assembly policy processes, coordination aspects, data usage accessibility principle data management procedure certain health data infrastructure ensure legal compliance, consistency good data quality throughout different stage data life cycle. Data processor: According Article 3 (12) Regulation (EU) 2018/1725, processor shall mean "a natural legal person, public authority, agency body process personal data behalf controller." essential element therefore processor act "on behalf controller" thus subject instructions.In cases, processor may choose process data himself, may recourse subcontractor process data behalf. practice, depend upon processor agreement entered controller. Data provider/holder: natural legal person, entity body health care sector, performing research relation sectors, well European Union institutions, bodies, office agency ha right obligation, theability make available, including register, provide, restrict access exchange certain data. Data quality: degree set inherent characteristic data fulfills requirements.Notes: requirement defined purpose processing hence data quality viewed word also fitness purpose. purpose use data, including primary use secondary use. purpose data protection, data quality refers set principle laid Article 5 GDPR Article 4 Regulation (EU) 2018/1725, namely: Lawfulness, fairness transparency Purpose limitation Data minimisation Accuracy Storage limitation Integrity confidentiality Data reuse: simple form data reuse using data way (i.e. starting original dataset, drawing different research inferences). data also repurposed used another intent (i.e. using data health insurance registry health monitoring, research). Data sharing: Provision data data controller data user purpose joint individual use shared data, based condition use, directly intermediary. Data subject: defined GDPR, data subject person identified, directly indirectly, particular reference identifier name, identification number, location data, online identifier one factor specific physical, physiological, genetic, mental, economic, cultural social identity natural person. Data user:A natural legal person/organisation ha lawful access certain personal non-personal data authorised use data commercial noncommercial purposes. Dataset: Collection data represented particular form. Datasets vary depending upon type intended use, collecting organization ha decided organize data upon collection. Dataset essentially heterogeneous term could made type collection type data. Data curator: person responsible quality FAIRness health-related data, make sure value data discovered accessible. role also considers possibility enriching data increasing quality. Importantly, data curator might play role regarding processors, e.g. responsible data hand. Dataset catalogue: collection datasets descriptions, arranged systematic manner consists user-oriented public part, information concerning individual dataset parameter accessible electronic mean online portal. Data steward: person ha administrative role; really use data. create guideline make data FAIR advice it. Stewards might direct responsibility data hand (processors) not. Distributed research infrastructure: decentralized organised network resources. FAIR Data principles: Principles define Findability, Accessibility, Interoperability, Reuse resource human computer source. example, principle emphasise machine-actionability (i.e., capacity computational system find, access, interoperate, reuse data none minimal human intervention) human increasingly rely computational support deal data result increase volume, complexity, creation speed data. Findable: Data supplementary material sufficiently rich metadata unique persistent identifier. Accessible: Metadata data understandable human machines. Data deposited trusted repository Interoperable: Metadata use formal, accessible, shared, broadly applicable language knowledge representation. Re-usable: Data collection clear usage license provide accurate information provenance. Federated data analysis: Federated data analysis describes analysis performed multiple (often geographically) separated datasets. analysis, data exchanged stay, example, behind given institution firewall. interim result local analysis exchanged data-hosting sites). aggregated non-identifiable result local analysis pooled returned data user. Federated database: Afederated database systemis type of(DBMS), transparently map multiple autonomousinto singlefederated database. constituentare interconnected via aand may geographically decentralized. Federated learning: specific case federated data analysis, machine learning purposes. learning technique allows user collectively reap benefit shared model trained rich data collections. learning task conducted across multiple separate site coordinated centrally. site ha local training dataset never shared . Instead, site computes update current global model maintained centrally, updated model communicated Health data: Personal data related physical mental health natural person, including provision health care services, reveal information health status.Health data collection: technical infrastructure hold datasets, make datasets available use, organises data logical manner. datasets may come different sources, hospital and/or research institute country (national data repositories) different country (international data repositories). Data collection may also cover appropriate, subject-specific location researcher submit data. Data collection may specific requirement concerning subject research domain; data reuse access; file format data structure; type metadata used. Minimal inclusion criteria: digital platform receives store data receives data single source and/or multiple source Allows discovery stored health data must control data stored possible characteristic data collection: could specific thematic, data type collect (e.g. particular disease, particular data type: genomic data, clinical data, EHRs) could part one overarching data hub could generate data Health data hub: Minimal inclusion criteria: digital technical infrastructure core mission enabling health data sharing provides health data different source allows discovery health datasets ha metadata discovery service ha data accessibility mechanism accordance existing regulation ha authorization functionality, provided Data Hub external institution. Health information: organised contextualised data population health health service activity performance, individual aggregated, improves health promotion, prevention, care policy-making. Health information systems: health information system total resources, stakeholders, activity output enabling evidence-informed health policy-making. health information system manages type health data, EHRs imaging data population health data. activity include: data collection, interpretation (analysis synthesis), health reporting, knowledge translation, i.e. stimulating enhancing uptake health information policy practice. Health information system governance relates mechanism process coordinate steer element health information system. : infodemic overabundance information accurate occurs epidemic. spread human similar manner epidemic, via digital physical information systems. make hard people find trustworthy source reliable guidance need it. Information: Data contextualised, i.e. reduced, summarized adjusted variation age sex population comparison time place possible. Infrastructure provider: responsible organisation support physical management health-related data following existing regulations. Parent definition data hub, data collection secure processing environment. Input Data: Data provided directly acquired AI system basis system produce output. Intelligence: product information transformed integration processing experience perception based social political values. Interoperability: Following European Interoperability Framework, interoperability refers a) full compliance legal ethical provision constituent node; b) organisation support knowledge exchange software transference across nodes; c) compatible technological environment support communication node allows deployment computational tasks; d) existence common data model enables semantic standardisation across data sources. distributed research infrastructure, interoperability key feature governance achievements. Knowledge translation: appropriate exchange, synthesis ethically sound application knowledge intervention strengthen healthcare system improve health. Machine learning: subset AI technique based use statistical mathematical modelling technique define analyse data. learned pattern applied perform guide certain task make predictions. Metadata: set data defines describes resource (e.g., data, dataset, sample...) understood, discovered reused. different level metadata. Since metadata used describe different aspect data, group metadata property term quality, availability, provenance, processing, among others. metadata catalogue developed describe available data collection repository hub. Metadata important make data understandable, contribute increase findability, accessibility, interoperability reusability data. Metadata collected compiled repository improve FAIRness level data collections. Mock-up data: Low quality synthetic data pattern correlation variable (i.e social factor depending area). Mock-up data used know real data look like, create analysis script. However, cannot used make real analysis (machine learning) reflect well real data*. National Node: ANational Node (NN) organisational entity, often linked national institution governmental unit function national liaison brings together relevant national stakeholder country systematic way. relevant stakeholder may include, example, national statistical office, national public health institutes, representative ministry health, research and/or science, others. addition, NN may function discussion advisory forum matter health data information national international matters. Examples include aspect governance data, indicator health reporting international level health information stakeholder national level. Non-personal data: data personal data. Open data: Data freely available everyone use republish wish, without restriction copyright, patent mechanism control. Open license license agreement contains provision allow individual reuse another creator's work, giving four major freedoms. Without special license, us normally prohibited copyright law commercial license. free license worldwide, royalty-free, non-exclusive, perpetual (see copyright durations). Free license often basis crowdsourcing crowdfunding projects. Open science: movement make scientific research (including publications, data, physical samples, software) dissemination accessible level inquiring society, amateur professional. Open science transparent accessible knowledge shared developed collaborative networks. encompasses practice publishing open research, campaigning open access, encouraging scientist practice open-notebook science, generally making easier publish communicate scientific knowledge. Personal data:According Article 3 (1) Regulation (EU) 2018/1725: "personal data mean information relating identified identifiable natural person (data subject); identifiable natural person one identified, directly indirectly, particular reference identifier name, identification number, location data, online identifier one factor specific physical, physiological, genetic, mental, economic, cultural social identity natural person".Name social security number two example personal data relate directly person. However, definition extends also encompasses instance e-mail address office phone number employee. example personal data found information physical disabilities, medical record employee's evaluation. Personal data processed relation work data subject remain personal/individual sense continue protected relevant data protection legislation, strives protect privacy integrity natural persons. consequence, data protection legislation doe address situation legal person (apart exceptional case information legal person also relates physical person). Personal data breach: breach security leading accidental unlawful destruction, loss, alteration, unauthorised disclosure of, access to, personal data transmitted, stored otherwise processed. Population Health Data/Health information: organised contextualised data health health service activity performance, individual population level, fit-for-use contributes health promotion, prevention, care policy-making. Primary use data: use data purpose wa originally collected. Processing (personal non-personal): operation set operation performed data datasets, whether automated means, collection, recording, organisation, structuring, storage, adaptation alteration, retrieval, consultation, use, disclosureby transmission, dissemination otherwise making available, alignment combination, restriction, erasure destruction. Profiling: form automated processing personal data consisting use personal data evaluate certain personal aspect relating natural person, particular analyse predict aspect concerning natural person's performance work, economic situation, health, personal preferences, interests, reliability, behaviour, location movements. Pseudonymisation: processing personal data manner personal data longer attributed specific data subject without use additional information, provided additional information kept separately subject technical organisational measure ensure personal data attributed identified identifiable natural person. Public health monitoring reporting: activity necessary obtain health data information bring information health policy practice. Research Network: Research Network (RN) active networkof national and/or regional expert several country perform comparative research specific health area (information domain). Restriction processing (personal non-personal data): defined GDPR, method restrict processing data could include, inter alia, temporarily moving selected data another processing system, making selected personal data unavailable users, temporarily removing published data website. automated filing systems, restriction processing principle ensured technical mean manner personal data subject processing operation cannot changed. fact processing data restricted clearly indicated system. Secondary use data/data re-use:Secondary use refers using data different purpose one wa originally collected (i.e. primary use). According European Data Governance Act 2020 re-use mean use natural legal person data held public sector bodies, commercial noncommercial purpose initial purpose within public task data produced, except exchange data public sector body purely pursuit public tasks. Clinical definition: Secondary use health data applies personal health information (PHI) us outside direct health care delivery. Secure processing environment: physical virtual environment organisational mean provide opportunity re-use data manner allows operator secure processing environment determine supervise data processing actions, including display, storage, download, export data calculation derivative data computational algorithms. Sensitive data: Information regulated law due possible risk plants, animals, individual and/or community public private organisations. Sensitive personal data include information related racial ethnic origin, political opinions, religious philosophical beliefs, trade union membership data concerning health sex life individual. data could identifiable potentially cause harm disclosure. Synthetic data:The concept synthetic data generation take original data source (dataset) create new, artificial data, similar statistical property it. Keeping statistical property mean anyone analysing synthetic data, data analyst example, able draw statistical conclusion analysis given dataset synthetic data he/she would given real (original) data. use synthetic data growing many fields: training artificial intelligence model within health sector computer vision, image recognition robotics fields. *Synthetic data confused "mockup data", which, although close, synonymous. Mockup data primarily used initial testing purposes, e.g. design phase prototype applications. doe necessarily maintain statistical property real data. Learn difference synthethic v mockup data . Testing Data: Data used providing independent evaluation trained validated AI system order confirm expected performance system placing market putting service. Training Data: Data used training machine learning algorithm (e.g., artificial intelligence (AI) system) fitting learnable parameters. Validation Data: Data used providing evaluation trained AI system tuning non-learnable parameter learning process.
